## Diagram 2

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
  participant Caller as fetchSearch Caller
  participant State as App State
  participant Duck as Search Duck
  participant WatchedDuck as watchedPackageListDuck
  participant DestDuck as destinationLocationsDuck
  participant Axios as axios
  participant Dispatcher as dispatch
  Caller->>State: call fetchSearch(queryString,...)
  State->>Caller: returns batchFilter
  alt batchFilter present
    Caller->>Dispatcher: invoke batchSearch(...)
    Dispatcher->>Axios: axios.post(batchSearchUrl, data, config)
    Axios-->>Dispatcher: response
    Dispatcher->>Duck: dispatch RECEIVE with transformSearchResponse(response.data)
    Dispatcher->>Dispatcher: dispatch OCEAN_TRACKING_SEARCH
  else no batchFilter
    Caller->>Dispatcher: build entitiesUrl and axiosConfig
    Dispatcher->>Duck: dispatch duck.fetch(url, config, transformSearchResponse)
    Dispatcher->>WatchedDuck: dispatch watchedPackageListDuck.fetch(url, config)
    Dispatcher->>Dispatcher: dispatch OCEAN_TRACKING_SEARCH (unless preventRedirect)
  end
```

stateDiagram-v2

  Received --> Redirected
  Error --> Idle
  Redirected --> Idle
